## Summary
<p>Pre-release for npm beta tag <code>v2026.3.22-beta.1</code>.</p>
<p>No new macOS app build is attached to this beta. macOS assets remain on stable app version <code>2026.3.22</code>, and <code>appcast.xml</code> is intentionally unchanged in this pre-release.</p>
<h3>Breaking</h3>
<ul>
<li>Plugins/install: bare <code>openclaw plugins install &lt;package&gt;</code> now prefers ClawHub before npm for npm-safe names, and only falls back to npm when ClawHub does not have that package or version. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/clawhub" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/clawhub</a></li>
<li>Browser/Chrome MCP: remove the legacy Chrome extension relay path, bundled extension assets, <code>driver: "extension"</code>, and <code>browser.relayBindHost</code>. Run <code>openclaw doctor --fix</code> to migrate host-local browser config to <code>existing-session</code> / <code>user</code>; Docker, headless, sandbox, and remote browser flows still use raw CDP. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/gateway/doctor" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/gateway/doctor</a> and <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/browser" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/browser</a> (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4080163403" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/47893" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/47893/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/47893">#47893</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Tools/image generation: standardize the stock image create/edit path on the core <code>image_generate</code> tool. The old <code>nano-banana-pro</code> docs/examples are gone; if you previously copied that sample-skill config, switch to <code>agents.defaults.imageGenerationModel</code> for built-in image generation or install a separate third-party skill explicitly.</li>
<li>Skills/image generation: remove the bundled <code>nano-banana-pro</code> skill wrapper. Use <code>agents.defaults.imageGenerationModel.primary: "google/gemini-3-pro-image-preview"</code> for the native Nano Banana-style path instead.</li>
<li>Plugins/SDK: the new public plugin SDK surface is <code>openclaw/plugin-sdk/*</code>; <code>openclaw/extension-api</code> is removed with no compatibility shim. Bundled plugins must use injected runtime for host-side operations (for example <code>api.runtime.agent.runEmbeddedPiAgent</code>) and any remaining direct imports must come from narrow <code>openclaw/plugin-sdk/*</code> subpaths instead of the monolithic SDK root. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-migration" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-migration</a> and <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-overview" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-overview</a></li>
<li>Plugins/message discovery: require <code>ChannelMessageActionAdapter.describeMessageTool(...)</code> for shared <code>message</code> tool discovery. The legacy <code>listActions</code>, <code>getCapabilities</code>, and <code>getToolSchema</code> adapter methods are removed. Plugin authors should migrate message discovery to <code>describeMessageTool(...)</code> and keep channel-specific action runtime code inside the owning plugin package. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/gumadeiras/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/gumadeiras">@gumadeiras</a>.</li>
<li>Plugins/Matrix: add a new Matrix plugin backed by the official <code>matrix-js-sdk</code>. If you are upgrading from the previous public Matrix plugin, follow the migration guide: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating-matrix" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating-matrix</a> Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/gumadeiras/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/gumadeiras">@gumadeiras</a>.</li>
<li>Config/env: remove legacy <code>CLAWDBOT_*</code> and <code>MOLTBOT_*</code> compatibility env names across runtime, installers, and test tooling. Use the matching <code>OPENCLAW_*</code> env names instead.</li>
<li>Config/state: remove legacy <code>.moltbot</code> state-dir and <code>moltbot.json</code> auto-detection/migration fallback. If you still keep state under <code>~/.moltbot</code>, move it to <code>~/.openclaw</code> or set <code>OPENCLAW_STATE_DIR</code> / <code>OPENCLAW_CONFIG_PATH</code> explicitly. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating</a> and <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/start/getting-started" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/start/getting-started</a></li>
<li>Exec/env sandbox: block build-tool JVM injection (<code>MAVEN_OPTS</code>, <code>SBT_OPTS</code>, <code>GRADLE_OPTS</code>, <code>ANT_OPTS</code>), glibc tunable exploitation (<code>GLIBC_TUNABLES</code>), and .NET dependency resolution hijack (<code>DOTNET_ADDITIONAL_DEPS</code>) from the host exec environment, and restrict Gradle init script redirect (<code>GRADLE_USER_HOME</code>) as an override-only block so user-configured Gradle homes still propagate. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4093859450" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/49702" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49702/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49702">#49702</a>)</li>
<li>Discord/commands: switch native command deployment to Carbon reconcile by default so Discord restarts stop churning slash commands through OpenClaw’s local deploy path. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4076819555" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/46597" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/46597/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/46597">#46597</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/huntharo/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/huntharo">@huntharo</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/thewilloftheshadow/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/thewilloftheshadow">@thewilloftheshadow</a>.</li>
<li>Security/exec approvals: treat <code>time</code> as a transparent dispatch wrapper during allowlist evaluation and allow-always persistence so approved <code>time ...</code> commands bind the inner executable instead of the wrapper path. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/YLChen-007/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/YLChen-007">@YLChen-007</a> for reporting.</li>
<li>Voice-call/webhooks: reject missing provider signature headers before body reads, drop the pre-auth body budget to <code>64 KB</code> / <code>5s</code>, and cap concurrent pre-auth requests per source IP so unauthenticated callers cannot force the old <code>1 MB</code> / <code>30s</code> buffering path. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/SEORY0/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/SEORY0">@SEORY0</a> for reporting.</li>
<li>Plugins/Matrix: stop mention-gated or otherwise dropped room chatter from refreshing focused thread bindings before the message is actually routed, so idle ACP and session bindings can still expire normally in mention-required rooms. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/dinakars777/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/dinakars777">@dinakars777</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/mvanhorn/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/mvanhorn">@mvanhorn</a>.</li>
<li>Plugins/Matrix: durably dedupe inbound room events across gateway restarts so previously handled Matrix messages are not replayed as new, while preserving clean-restart backlog delivery for unseen events. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4106443066" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/50922" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/50922/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/50922">#50922</a>) thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/gumadeiras/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/gumadeiras">@gumadeiras</a></li>
<li>Agents/media replies: migrate the remaining browser, canvas, and nodes snapshot outputs onto <code>details.media</code> so generated media keeps attaching to assistant replies after the collect-then-attach refactor. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4112978317" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/51731" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/51731/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/51731">#51731</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/christianklotz/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/christianklotz">@christianklotz</a>.</li>
<li>Android/contacts search: escape literal <code>%</code> and <code>_</code> in contact-name queries so searches like <code>100%</code> or <code>_id</code> no longer match unrelated contacts through SQL <code>LIKE</code> wildcards. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4049922961" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/41891" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/41891/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/41891">#41891</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/Kaneki-x/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/Kaneki-x">@Kaneki-x</a>.</li>
<li>Gateway/usage: include reset and deleted archived session transcripts in usage totals, session discovery, and archived-only session detail fallback so the Usage view no longer undercounts rotated sessions. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4058275801" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/43215" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/43215/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/43215">#43215</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/rcrick/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/rcrick">@rcrick</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>ClawHub/install: add native <code>openclaw skills search|install|update</code> flows plus <code>openclaw plugins install clawhub:&lt;package&gt;</code> with tracked update metadata, gateway skill-install/update support for ClawHub-backed requests, and regression coverage/docs for the new source path.</li>
<li>Plugins/marketplaces: add Claude marketplace registry resolution, <code>plugin@marketplace</code> installs, marketplace listing, and update support, plus Docker E2E coverage for local and official marketplace flows. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4081070651" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/48058" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/48058/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/48058">#48058</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Commands/plugins: add owner-gated <code>/plugins</code> and <code>/plugin</code> chat commands for plugin list/show and enable/disable flows, alongside explicit <code>commands.plugins</code> config gating. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Install/update: allow package-manager installs from GitHub <code>main</code> via <code>openclaw update --tag main</code>, installer <code>--version main</code>, or direct npm/pnpm git specs. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4079200109" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/47630" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/47630/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/47630">#47630</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Plugins/bundles: add compatible Codex, Claude, and Cursor bundle discovery/install support, map bundle skills into OpenClaw skills, and apply Claude bundle <code>settings.json</code> defaults to embedded Pi with shell overrides sanitized.</li>
<li>CLI/hooks: route hook-pack install and update through <code>openclaw plugins</code>, keep <code>openclaw hooks</code> focused on hook visibility and per-hook controls, and show plugin-managed hook details in CLI output.</li>
<li>Models/OpenAI: switch the default OpenAI setup model to <code>openai/gpt-5.4</code>, keep Codex on <code>openai-codex/gpt-5.4</code>, and centralize OpenAI chat, image, TTS, transcription, and embedding defaults in one shared module so future default-model updates stay low-churn. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Agents: add per-agent thinking/reasoning/fast defaults and auto-revert disallowed model overrides to the agent's default selection. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/xuanmingguo/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/xuanmingguo">@xuanmingguo</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Commands/btw: add <code>/btw</code> side questions for quick tool-less answers about the current session without changing future session context, with dismissible in-session TUI answers and explicit BTW replies on external channels. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4073288843" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/45444" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/45444/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/45444">#45444</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ngutman/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ngutman">@ngutman</a>.</li>

<li>Sandbox/SSH: add a core SSH sandbox backend with secret-backed key, certificate, and known_hosts inputs, move shared remote exec/filesystem tooling into core, and keep OpenShell focused on sandbox lifecycle plus optional <code>mirror</code> mode.</li>
<li>Browser/existing-session: support <code>browser.profiles.&lt;name&gt;.userDataDir</code> so Chrome DevTools MCP can attach to Brave, Edge, and other Chromium-based browsers through their own user data directories. <li>Control UI/appearance: unify theme border radii across Claw, Knot, and Dash, and add a Roundness slider to the Appearance settings so users can adjust corner radius from sharp to fully rounded. <h3>Fixes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Web tools/search provider lists: keep onboarding, configure, and docs provider lists alphabetical while preserving the separate runtime auto-detect precedence used for credential-based provider selection.</li>
<li>Media/Windows security: block remote-host <code>file://</code> media URLs and UNC/network paths before local filesystem resolution in core media loading and adjacent prompt/sandbox attachment seams, so the next release no longer allows structured local-media inputs to trigger outbound SMB credential handshakes on Windows. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/RacerZ-fighting/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/RacerZ-fighting">@RacerZ-fighting</a> for reporting.</li>
<li>Gateway/discovery: fail closed on unresolved Bonjour and DNS-SD service endpoints in CLI discovery, onboarding, and <code>gateway status</code> so TXT-only hints can no longer steer routing or SSH auto-target selection. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nexrin/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nexrin">@nexrin</a> for reporting.</li>
<li>Security/pairing: bind iOS setup codes to the intended node profile and reject first-use bootstrap redemption that asks for broader roles or scopes. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/tdjackey/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/tdjackey">@tdjackey</a>.</li>
<li>Memory/core tools: register <code>memory_search</code> and <code>memory_get</code> independently so one unavailable memory tool no longer suppresses the other in new sessions. ## Why It Matters
Source signal: <p>Pre-release for npm beta tag <code>v2026.3.22-beta.1</code>.</p>
<p>No new macOS app build is attached to this beta. macOS assets remain on stable app version <code>2026.3.22</code>, and <code>appcast.xml</code> is intentionally unchanged in this pre-release.</p>
<h3>Breaking</h3>
<ul>
<li>Plugins/install: bare <code>openclaw plugins install &lt;package&gt;</code> now prefers ClawHub before npm for npm-safe names, and only falls back to npm when ClawHub does not have that package or version. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/clawhub" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/clawhub</a></li>
<li>Browser/Chrome MCP: remove the legacy Chrome extension relay path, bundled extension assets, <code>driver: "extension"</code>, and <code>browser.relayBindHost</code>. Run <code>openclaw doctor --fix</code> to migrate host-local browser config to <code>existing-session</code> / <code>user</code>; Docker, headless, sandbox, and remote browser flows still use raw CDP. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/gateway/doctor" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/gateway/doctor</a> and <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/browser" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/tools/browser</a> (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4080163403" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/47893" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/47893/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/47893">#47893</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Tools/image generation: standardize the stock image create/edit path on the core <code>image_generate</code> tool. The old <code>nano-banana-pro</code> docs/examples are gone; if you previously copied that sample-skill config, switch to <code>agents.defaults.imageGenerationModel</code> for built-in image generation or install a separate third-party skill explicitly.</li>
<li>Skills/image generation: remove the bundled <code>nano-banana-pro</code> skill wrapper. Use <code>agents.defaults.imageGenerationModel.primary: "google/gemini-3-pro-image-preview"</code> for the native Nano Banana-style path instead.</li>
<li>Plugins/SDK: the new public plugin SDK surface is <code>openclaw/plugin-sdk/*</code>; <code>openclaw/extension-api</code> is removed with no compatibility shim. Bundled plugins must use injected runtime for host-side operations (for example <code>api.runtime.agent.runEmbeddedPiAgent</code>) and any remaining direct imports must come from narrow <code>openclaw/plugin-sdk/*</code> subpaths instead of the monolithic SDK root. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-migration" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-migration</a> and <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-overview" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/plugins/sdk-overview</a></li>
<li>Plugins/message discovery: require <code>ChannelMessageActionAdapter.describeMessageTool(...)</code> for shared <code>message</code> tool discovery. The legacy <code>listActions</code>, <code>getCapabilities</code>, and <code>getToolSchema</code> adapter methods are removed. Plugin authors should migrate message discovery to <code>describeMessageTool(...)</code> and keep channel-specific action runtime code inside the owning plugin package. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/gumadeiras/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/gumadeiras">@gumadeiras</a>.</li>
<li>Plugins/Matrix: add a new Matrix plugin backed by the official <code>matrix-js-sdk</code>. If you are upgrading from the previous public Matrix plugin, follow the migration guide: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating-matrix" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating-matrix</a> Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/gumadeiras/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/gumadeiras">@gumadeiras</a>.</li>
<li>Config/env: remove legacy <code>CLAWDBOT_*</code> and <code>MOLTBOT_*</code> compatibility env names across runtime, installers, and test tooling. Use the matching <code>OPENCLAW_*</code> env names instead.</li>
<li>Config/state: remove legacy <code>.moltbot</code> state-dir and <code>moltbot.json</code> auto-detection/migration fallback. If you still keep state under <code>~/.moltbot</code>, move it to <code>~/.openclaw</code> or set <code>OPENCLAW_STATE_DIR</code> / <code>OPENCLAW_CONFIG_PATH</code> explicitly. Docs: <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/install/migrating</a> and <a href="https://docs.openclaw.ai/start/getting-started" rel="nofollow">https://docs.openclaw.ai/start/getting-started</a></li>
<li>Exec/env sandbox: block build-tool JVM injection (<code>MAVEN_OPTS</code>, <code>SBT_OPTS</code>, <code>GRADLE_OPTS</code>, <code>ANT_OPTS</code>), glibc tunable exploitation (<code>GLIBC_TUNABLES</code>), and .NET dependency resolution hijack (<code>DOTNET_ADDITIONAL_DEPS</code>) from the host exec environment, and restrict Gradle init script redirect (<code>GRADLE_USER_HOME</code>) as an override-only block so user-configured Gradle homes still propagate. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4093859450" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/49702" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49702/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49702">#49702</a>)</li>
<li>Discord/commands: switch native command deployment to Carbon reconcile by default so Discord restarts stop churning slash commands through OpenClaw’s local deploy path. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4076819555" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/46597" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/46597/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/46597">#46597</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/huntharo/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/huntharo">@huntharo</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/thewilloftheshadow/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/thewilloftheshadow">@thewilloftheshadow</a>.</li>

<h3>Fixes</h3>
<ul>
<li>Web tools/search provider lists: keep onboarding, configure, and docs provider lists alphabetical while preserving the separate runtime auto-detect precedence used for credential-based provider selection.</li>
<li>Media/Windows security: block remote-host <code>file://</code> media URLs and UNC/network paths before local filesystem resolution in core media loading and adjacent prompt/sandbox attachment seams, so the next release no longer allows structured local-media inputs to trigger outbound SMB credential handshakes on Windows. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/RacerZ-fighting/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/RacerZ-fighting">@RacerZ-fighting</a> for reporting.</li>
<li>Gateway/discovery: fail closed on unresolved Bonjour and DNS-SD service endpoints in CLI discovery, onboarding, and <code>gateway status</code> so TXT-only hints can no longer steer routing or SSH auto-target selection. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nexrin/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nexrin">@nexrin</a> for reporting.</li>
<li>Security/pairing: bind iOS setup codes to the intended node profile and reject first-use bootstrap redemption that asks for broader roles or scopes. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/tdjackey/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/tdjackey">@tdjackey</a>.</li>
<li>Memory/core tools: register <code>memory_search</code> and <code>memory_get</code> independently so one unavailable memory tool no longer suppresses the other in new sessions. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4099220942" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/50198" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/50198/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/50198">#50198</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/artwalker/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/artwalker">@artwalker</a>.</li>
